<spectrum-accordion data-name="FAQ5"><div class="spectrum-Accordion FAQ5" role="region"><div class="spectrum-Accordion-item react-spectrum-Accordion-item" role="presentation"><h3 class="spectrum-Accordion-itemHeading" aria-level="3"><button id="react-spectrum-10" class="spectrum-Accordion-itemHeader" aria-controls="react-spectrum-11" aria-expanded="false" type="button">Can I import 3D models into Substance 3D Modeler?</button><svg class="spectrum-UIIcon-ChevronRightMedium spectrum-Icon spectrum-Accordion-itemIndicator" focusable="false" aria-hidden="true" role="presentation"><path d="M5.99 5a1 1 0 0 0-.29-.707L1.717.3A1 1 0 1 0 .3 1.717L3.586 5 .3 8.283A1 1 0 1 0 1.717 9.7L5.7 5.707A1 1 0 0 0 5.99 5z" class="spectrum-UIIcon--medium"></path><path d="M7.5 6a1 1 0 0 0-.293-.707L2.217.3A1 1 0 1 0 .8 1.717L5.086 6 .8 10.283A1 1 0 1 0 2.217 11.7l4.99-4.99A1 1 0 0 0 7.5 6z" class="spectrum-UIIcon--large"></path></svg></h3><div id="react-spectrum-11" role="region" aria-labelledby="react-spectrum-10" aria-hidden="true" aria-expanded="false" class="spectrum-Accordion-itemContent"><div class="item-CanIimport3DmodelsintoSubstance3DModeler-FAQ5">


<div class="aem-Grid aem-Grid--12 aem-Grid--default--12 ">
    
    <div class="text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">

    
     
     
    
        <div class="cmp-text body-XS">

            <p>To import a mesh into Modeler, use the File &gt; Import Mesh option in the menu, or the shortcut ctrl + shift + m. Modeler supports most standard file types, including OBJ, FBX, USD, and glTF. You can also import any Modeler scene which is saved as an SMOD file.</p>

        </div>
    


    

</div>

    
</div>
</div></div></div></div></spectrum-accordion>
